***ревизия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ревизия.html>реви́зия</a> (14661)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">rewizja</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">revīsiō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">review</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; original meaning "census of the male population". From the time of Peter I.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревизия.html>реви́зия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">revízija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревизия.html>реви́зии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревизия.html>реви́зии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревизия.html>реви́зий</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ревизио́нный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>audit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">independent review</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> inspection, examination</li>
<li>revision <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a theory or treaty</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> census of the male population <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">for calculating poll taxes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>tax roll, tax register</li></ol>

***ревнитель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ревнитель.html>ревни́тель</a> (21821)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Constructed as if <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*ревни́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*revnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревновать.html>ревнова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">revnovátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be jealous, <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to be zealous</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревнитель.html>ревни́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">revnítelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревнитель.html>ревни́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревнитель.html>ревни́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревнитель.html>ревни́телей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ревни́тельница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary or high-style</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> zealot, strict adherent, ardent advocate</li></ol>

***ревновать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ревновать.html>ревнова́ть</a> (8952)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ревн-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">revn-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревновать.html>ревнова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">revnovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be jealous of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ревновать.html>ревну́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:коллега.html>колле́гам</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On částo <b>revnújet</b> jejó k jejó kollégam.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He is often jealous of her colleagues because of her.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to envy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ревновать.html>ревнова́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ве</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>revnovátʹ</b> sláve svojevó drúga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to envy one's friend's fame</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be zealous (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> about something)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to compete (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with someone)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ревность.html>ре́вность</a> (6491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">рьвение</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rĭvenie</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">strife, quarrel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">rzewniwy</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">ревни́вий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">revnývyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реветь.html>реве́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">revétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревность.html>ре́вность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">révnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревность.html>ре́вности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревность.html>ре́вности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревность.html>ре́вностей</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ревнуемый.html>ревну́емый</a> (8952)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревнуемый.html>ревну́емый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">revnújemyj</span>)
</p>

</p>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:революционный.html>революцио́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:продукт.html>проду́кт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>revoljuciónnyj</b> prodúkt</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>revolutionary</b> product</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:революция.html>револю́ция</a> (819)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">rewolucja</i>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">revolutio</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:революция.html>револю́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">revoljúcija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:революция.html>револю́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:революция.html>револю́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:революция.html>револю́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>revolution <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">political upheaval</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:регенерация.html>регенера́ция</a> (24159)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">regenerātiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регенерация.html>регенера́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">regenerácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регенерация.html>регенера́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регенерация.html>регенера́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регенерация.html>регенера́ций</a></b>)
</p>

***регистратор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:регистратор.html>регистра́тор</a> (21894)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">registrator</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регистратор.html>регистра́тор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">registrátor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регистратор.html>регистра́тора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регистратор.html>регистра́торы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регистратор.html>регистра́торов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> registrar, recordkeeper, file clerk</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hospital receptionist</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> recorder, recording device</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> logger</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> display, monitor</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> file, folder</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регистрировать.html>регистри́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">registrírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p>Probably <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регламент.html>регла́мент</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">regláment</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***регулировавшийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:регулироваться.html>регули́ровавшийся</a> (29800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:регулировать.html>регули́ровать</a> (11276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регулировать.html>регули́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">regulírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрегулировать.html>отрегули́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to regulate, to control</li>
<li>to adjust, to tune up</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:регулировка.html>регулиро́вка</a> (27274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регулировать.html>регули́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">regulírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регулировка.html>регулиро́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">reguliróvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регулировка.html>регулиро́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регулировка.html>регулиро́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регулировка.html>регулиро́вок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>adjustment, readjustment <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">small change</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>control, regulation</li>
<li>alignment, aligning</li>
<li>tuning, tune-up</li></ol>
